contentSet="News" majVers="1" minVers="3.0"><ContentItem xsi:type="news:NewsDataItem"><newsItem standard="NewsML-G2" standardversion="2.7" conformance="power" guid="20151001-000000000-nL3T1202PU-1-2" version="1" xml:lang="en" xsi:schemaLocation="http://iptc.org/std/nar/2006-10-01/ NAR_1.8-spec-All-Power_2.xsd http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml xhtml1-strict.xsd" xmlns="http://iptc.org/std/nar/2006-10-01/" xmlns:rtr="http://www.reuters.com/ns/2003/08/content" xmlns:x="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><catalogRef href="http://www.iptc.org/std/catalog/catalog.IPTC-G2-Standards_14.xml" /><itemMeta><itemClass rtr:isOriginal="1">nL3T1202PU</altId><language tag="zh" /><subject qcode="N2:STX" /><subject qcode="N2:COM" /><subject qcode="N2:CYCS" /><subject qcode="N2:AUTO" /><subject qcode="N2:DIV" /><subject qcode="N2:RES" /><subject qcode="N2:EMRG" /><subject qcode="N2:TW" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:COPINI" /><subject qcode="N2:BACT" /><subject qcode="N2:LZH" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>專欄節選：9月22日這一天，全球跑出三隻黑天鵝--今周刊「老謝開講」</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body> (本文由台灣《今周刊》雜誌提供,節選自10月1日出版的當期「老謝開講」專欄)
嘉能可崩壞凸顯了中國經濟風險，福斯重創德國經濟，希拉蕊意外戳破美國生技股泡沫，這三隻黑天鵝一起飛出來，鐵定對今年全球股市與經濟帶來重大衝擊與影響。

    美國聯準會(Fed)主席葉倫九月宣布暫不升息，給全球經濟帶來不安的聯想，正當全球投資人對未來充滿悲觀預期的關鍵時刻，天空上飛出了三隻黑天鵝，為全世界經濟帶來更多不安定的元素。

    **三隻新黑天鵝，為世界經濟帶來不安**

    這三隻新黑天鵝意外都出現在九月二十二日前後，分別是美國總統參選人希拉蕊意外推倒氣勢如虹、勢不可擋的當紅炸子雞生技股；第二隻黑天鵝是福斯汽車作弊案重創了以嚴謹製造得到世界肯定的德國製造業，也讓德國股市一直沉淪；第三隻黑天鵝是貴金屬交易商嘉能可(Glencore)，這家在倫敦及香港掛牌的資源股，今年以來股價已重挫七五．五一％，未來還得面對三○○億美元的債務重組問題。嘉能可背後代表的是中國經濟的不振與原物料價格的跌跌不休。

    九月二十八日中國公布新的官方數據，八月中國工業生產的利潤率比去年同期大減八．八％，比前一個月減少二．九％，股票經紀商Interactive Investor衍生性商品主管Mike McCudden發文表示：「中國經濟數據持續令人失望，投資人信心又破滅了。」當天，道瓊指數大跌三三一．三七％，勉強守住一萬六千點，道瓊指數今年以來已下挫一○．二二％，被福斯拖累的德國股市也大跌二○四．九八點，也把今年的漲幅全都跌光。

    三隻新黑天鵝同時在天空飛翔，全球股市恐怕會籠罩在很低的低氣壓中。首先來看希拉蕊意外壓倒的生技股。

    九月二十一日，美國民主黨總統參選人希拉蕊在推特中推文表示，美國新藥藥價太貴，她將以實際行動對付藥廠敲竹杠的行為。

    被希拉蕊推到的兇手是美國新創生技公司圖靈製藥(Turing Pharmaceuticals)，將已上市六十二年的寄生蟲感染用藥Daraprim從原來每錠十三．五美元拉高到七五○美元，引起美國輿論撻伐，圖靈是在今年八月以五五○○萬美元買下Daraprim的專利權，Daraprim藥價驚人暴漲，讓希拉蕊有出手的機會，她果真在九月二十二日提出抑制處方用藥價格的方案。她提出的措施，包括：進口比較便宜的藥品，允許聯邦政府直接與藥商談判議價，以及規定製藥廠要以一定比率的利潤挹注研發，而不是列為報稅扣除成本項目的廣告開支。希拉蕊揚言要全力對付藥廠敲竹杠的行為。

    由於希拉蕊是民主黨呼聲最高的參選人，而且，二○一六年總統大選當選機率最大，她這一大聲疾呼，整個美國生技產業大大受到衝擊。九月二十一日美國生技股大跌一六四．四二點，跌幅達四．四％，希拉蕊打蛇打七寸，這一招正好命中美股要害。

    從金融海嘯以來，聯準會透過QE(貨幣量化寬鬆)，創造美股大牛市，道瓊指數從六四六九．九五點漲到一八三五一．三六點，大漲一八三％，標普五○○從六六二．九二點漲到二一三四．七二點，大漲二二二％，那斯達克從一二六五．五二點漲到五二三一．九四點，漲幅是三一三％；但是日正當中的生技股漲幅更驚人，NBI生技分類指數從五九○．二六點漲到四一九四．八七點，漲幅高達六．一倍，美國生技產業不斷創造一顆新藥傳奇，像美國藥廠吉利德科學（Gilead Sciences）的C型肝炎口服用藥Harvoni，一顆藥要價一一二五美元，引來外界批評。

    美國的資本市場在二○○○年上演的是科網傳奇，但是金融海嘯後，真正的創業傳奇都在生技產業上演。從嬌生、輝瑞、羅氏大藥廠、諾華藥廠、吉利德科學、諾和諾德、美國安進公司（AMGEN），必治妥、禮來等等，過去六年來股價漲幅都十分驚人，像嬌生市值一度突破三○○○億美元，輝瑞也突破二○○○億美元，美國生技業成為全球不斷超越顛峰、最佳淘金的產業。
 

    **希拉蕊出招，對付藥廠敲竹杠行為**

    這次希拉蕊提出的政見，衝擊生技產業最大的是藥廠不得將成本列為廣告支出；其次，她為聯邦政府對慢性病或有嚴重健康問題的病患，訂出每月二五○美元的處方藥實報實銷的成本上限，以限制保險公司要求病人負擔的金額，都對美國生技產業帶來重大衝擊。

    希拉蕊在選舉造勢大會上說：「我們必須保護勤奮工作的美國人，使他們免于承擔過重的成本，這些藥物往往耗費巨大，壓垮了家庭生計。」
    
    她進一步表示，藥廠為自己留住利潤，但不可以將成本漫無限制轉嫁給一般家庭。如果藥廠無法繼續將廣告支出列為減稅項目，聯邦政府將獲得可觀稅收。她認為，這個構想還可以補強歐巴馬總統正全力推動的全民健保法案。

    希拉蕊的抑制處方藥價格方案，得到民眾很大回響，但業者仍心存懷疑，因為相關法案過去二十年在國會都無法通過；不過，希拉蕊是美國最有勝算的總統參選人，她登高一呼，正好意外戳破美國生技大夢。美國生技股從九月二十一日大跌後，此後連續七個交易日重挫，最慘的是九月二十五日大跌五．○五％，九月二十八日大跌一九五．二八點，跌幅高達六．○二％。從希拉蕊提出藥價改革方案以來，美國NBI生技分類指數從三八三一．七九點跌到二九八九．○四點，跌幅超過二二％。生技股未來是美國最牛的產業，今年以來最大漲幅一度超過三二％，且今年已出現四％的跌幅。希拉蕊意外戳破美國生技股大泡沫，以及葉倫不升息引來大家對全球經濟黯淡的想像，今年美國股市可能要面臨○八年金融海嘯以來最寒冷冬天的考驗，對美股衝擊非同小可。
 

    **用軟體偽造排放數據，福斯金字招牌蒙塵**  

    全球金融市場的第二隻黑天鵝，是福斯汽車生產的柴油車以加裝作弊的軟體排放廢氣，在美國被戳破，福斯可能要面臨美國一八○億美元的罰款。福斯排廢造假，除了重傷福斯汽車股價，更重要的可能打擊德國一向給人嚴謹形象的製造業，傷害德國經濟。

    福斯汽車威力有多大？去年全球賣出八八○○萬輛汽車，福斯售出一五○○萬輛，占全球一七％，福斯旗下有眾多品牌，除了VW外，還有奧迪，著名跑車如賓利、保時捷、藍寶堅尼等，都出自福斯旗下。今年福斯汽車股價一度漲到二六九．二五歐元，市值達一四八五億歐元，福斯是德國最大汽車廠，也是德國最大企業雇主，單是雇用自德國本土的員工就超過二十七萬人，福斯在全球從業人員超過七十七．五萬人。汽車是德國最重要的支柱產業，一四年單是德國銷售及出口的產值即達三六八○億歐元，占ＧＤＰ(國內生產毛額)二．七％，而德國出口的汽車及零組件占出口額兩成，怪不得國際媒體稱，福斯危機可能比希臘危機更可怕。

    這次福斯危機除了傷到自己的形象，福斯股價一路重挫到一○六歐元，市值一度跌破六○○億歐元，如果從高價來算，市值約去掉三分之二。但更可怕的是福斯讓德國製造蒙上陰影，德國的製造業一向給人嚴謹可信賴的形象，這回這麼大的汽車廠居然也作弊，這對德國傷害太大了。
這個事件爆發後，福斯六十八歲的執行長溫特康(Martin Winterkorn)宣布去職，德國總理梅克爾也呼籲要透明處理此事，但福斯災難恐難善了。
    
    美國最大汽車經銷商AUTONATION總裁杰克遜（Mike Jackson）說，福斯在美國的品牌地位岌岌可危，預料福斯公司未來十年的銷售都會受影響，惠譽已表示，可能調降福斯的債信評等，德意志也把福斯汽車從「買入」降為「持有」。

    福斯作弊事件意外引來全球汽車股拋售潮，九月二十二日ＢＭＷ、賓士、標致雪鐵龍，及日本豐田、本田、日產等跌幅都逾五％，福斯則面臨商譽損失、品牌打折、股價市值大蒸發及高額罰單的善後成本，最糟的是衝擊德國經濟。今年德國股市一度大漲到一二三九○點，如今已跌破九五○○點關卡。福斯造假事件震驚全球，一家堪稱偉大的德國企業陷入暴風眼，而這不僅僅是福斯的危機，也是整個歐洲汽車業的危機，連「德國製造」的金字招牌也蒙塵。

    這次一一○○萬輛柴油車作假，可能拖累整個柴油車產業。與汽油車相比，柴油車每公里耗油和產生的二氧化碳都比較少，但柴油車製造的氮氧化物（NOx）較高，吸入會傷害肺部健康。歐洲從九二年開始制定廢氣排放標準，且愈來愈嚴格，就是為了確保車廠能製造出「潔凈引擎」，過濾有害物質，這是這些年歐洲政府以補貼獎勵生產柴油車的背景。歐洲的柴油車比率高得嚇人，反而在美國市占率不到四％。十五年來歐洲車廠投資柴油技術花了上百億歐元，這次作弊事件可能使柴油車產業蒙塵，也可能連帶拖累白金價格，白金用作柴油車催化轉換器(catalytic converter)中的催化劑，能減少汽車廢氣中的有害成分。今年白金需求八三一萬盎司，有四四％來自汽車減排裝置，這次福斯醜聞，可能進一步衝擊白金需求。
    

    **嘉能可股價崩跌，商品市場拉警報**

    另一個也是出現在九月二十二日的瑞士國際商品巨頭嘉能可股價瞬間暴跌二○％，這有如對全球大宗商品扔下一顆大炸彈。嘉能可是總部設在瑞士的全球最龐大的大宗商品寡頭貿易商，經手九十多項大宗商品，倫敦金屬交易所進行交割的鎳和鋁，有五○％到九○％都掌握在嘉能可手中，一四年被《FORTUNE》評選為全球五百大企業的第十名，排名還在蘋果前面。

    一一年嘉能可在倫敦與香港兩地上市，倫敦的嘉能可以每股五三○便士掛牌，發行一二．五億股，引入包括黑石、新加坡政府投資公司、瑞銀、瑞士信貸及福建紫金礦業等大股東。但是，中國經濟持續走緩，大宗商品價格已持續六年下跌，嘉能可上半年虧損六．七六億美元，相較於去年上半年獲利十七．二億美元，形成強烈對比。嘉能可同時宣布到明年底前還要削減三○○億美元債務的三分之一，包括停止到一五年終止的股息及出售二十億美元資產。今年以來，嘉能可股價持續走低，九月二十二日重挫到一二二．八便士，在香港掛牌的嘉能可股價也從四十三港幣跌到八．六八港幣，單是在香港，今年跌幅就達七六％，在香港掛牌的嘉能可九月二十九日重挫二九．三二％。

    嘉能可陷入困境，這與中國因素有關，《紐約時報》指稱，由於中國經濟放緩，中國將不再像過去那樣是大宗商品的主導力量，中國經濟未來的不確定性增加，嘉能可和全球大宗商品的命運會比以往更險峻。目前嘉能可處在虧損狀態，債務壓力更沉重，為了挽救自己的命運，嘉能可能進一步拋售手上持有的大宗商品，未來銅、錫、鋅可能面臨更大下跌風險。
嘉能可崩壞凸顯了中國經濟風險，福斯重創德國經濟，希拉蕊意外戳破美國生技股泡沫，這三隻黑天鵝一起飛出來，鐵定對今年全球股市與經濟帶來重大衝擊與影響。(完)

      註: 1.專欄作者老謝--謝金河，為《今周刊》發行人兼財訊文化事業執行長。
      2.以上評論不代表路透立場。

xsi:type="news:NewsDataItem"><newsItem standard="NewsML-G2" standardversion="2.7" conformance="power" guid="20151001-000000000-nL3T1203G5-1-2" version="1" xml:lang="en" qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" /><rtr:versionedId guid="20151001-000000000-nL3T1203G5-1-2" /><instanceOf qcode="NI:TW/ECICN" /><TakeSequence>1</TakeSequence></itemMeta><contentMeta><urgency>3</urgency><altId type="idType:USN" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL3T1203G5</altId><language tag="zh" /><subject qcode="N2:PREV" /><subject qcode="N2:ECI" /><subject qcode="N2:MCE" /><subject qcode="N2:EMRG" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:TW" /><subject qcode="N2:DIARY" /><subject qcode="N2:LZH" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>台灣經濟指標預測--10月1日至11月20日</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>以下為台灣近期預定公布的經濟數據：

<ContentEnvelope majVers="1" minVers="0.7" pubStyle="Message" xmlns="http://data.schemas.tfn.thomson.com/Envelope/2008-05-01/" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" contentSet="News" majVers="1" minVers="3.0"><ContentItem action="Insert"><Entitlements><Product><Code>NP:CLN</Code><Code>NP:PMF</Code><Code>NP:CMN</Code><Code>NP:DNP</Code><Code>NP:CDS</Code></Product><Source><Group>NONE</Group></Source></Entitlements><Data xsi:type="news:NewsDataItem"><newsItem standard="NewsML-G2" standardversion="2.7" conformance="power" guid="20151001-000000000-nL3T1203TJ-1-2" version="1" xml:lang="en" xsi:schemaLocation="http://iptc.org/std/nar/2006-10-01/ NAR_1.8-spec-All-Power_2.xsd http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml xhtml1-strict.xsd" xmlns="http://iptc.org/std/nar/2006-10-01/" xmlns:rtr="http://www.reuters.com/ns/2003/08/content" xmlns:x="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><catalogRef href="http://www.iptc.org/std/catalog/catalog.IPTC-G2-Standards_14.xml" /><itemMeta><itemClass qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" qcode="N2:LZH" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><subject qcode="R:TPITWDOND=" /><subject qcode="R:PIBC" /><headline>重溫稿--台灣貨幣市場：隔拆利率走揚，颱風假打亂季底調度節奏</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    * 颱風假打亂季底調度節奏
    * 隔拆利率走揚且取得不易
    * 短票與RP利率大致持穩

     記者 董永年
    路透台北9月30日 - 台灣銀行短率周三穩中趨揚。資金調度人士指出，今日適逢季底，
但碰巧昨日杜鵑颱風來襲金融市場暫停交易，使得調度節奏大亂，不少銀行保守因應，不願
拆出資金，令隔夜拆款利率走揚。
    
    他們表示，利率較高的短票與債市附買回(RP)交易較無影響，上午10點過後陸續有資金
釋出，不過拆款就要等到下午才會比較明確。由於整體資金相當寬裕，預料不致出現調度無
門的窘況。
    
    〞拆款優先，利率好談。〞一位大型票券商資調人士說。
    
    另一大型銀行交易主管則稱，中秋假期與颱風假共累積四天的交割必須處理，而且正好
遇到季底，因此各家銀行都相當保守，因此要等到稍晚才會放出資金。
    
    杜鵑(DUJUAN)颱風侵襲台灣，台北市政府宣布，周二(29日)全日停止上班，台灣金融市
場包括股市、期市、債市和匯市休市一日，交割順延。[nL3T11Y4C2]    
    
    
                              今日報價                 上日收盤
 隔夜銀行間拆款加權平均        0.313%                   0.302%
 利率                                         
 &lt;PIBC&gt;&lt;TPITWDOND=&gt;                           
   --隔夜拆款利率區間       0.270-0.340%             0.270-0.350%
   --一周拆款利率區間       0.300-0.440%             0.300-0.440%      
                                              
   --兩周拆款利率區間       0.300-0.430%             0.370-0.430%       
 
               
    **短票發行大增**
   
    短票方面，票券商交易員表示，由於累積了兩天，今日發票數量明顯增加，不過銀行端
市況紊亂，買票需求預估要等到下午才會放大。

    也有票券商交易員稱，由於昨日放颱風假，今日新發行的短票要等到下午才能銷售，如
此將延誤交割，因此只能賣庫存或是昨日發行的短票。        
  
    〞銀行市況很亂，每家資金計算方式不一樣。〞一位大型票券公司交易主管說。    
        
    大型票券商與銀行間承作的自保30天跨季短票主要成交在0.43%；60天期、90天期短票
分別成交在0.44%、0.45%。
    
    據集保的資料顯示，不分承作對象，上日30天自保短票次級買賣斷平均成交利率落在0.
435%，前日在0.463%；上日成交量148.09億台幣，前日125.39億台幣。
    
    台灣央行周三共發行5,307.5億台幣定存單，與今日存單到期金額5,308億台幣相較，存
單發行餘額減0.5億台幣。周四央行存單到期金額1,227.7億台幣、周五267億。  
    
    拆款中心資料&lt;PIBC&gt;顯示，周三超額準備為271億台幣，累積超額準備為8,473億台幣、
加計前期1%的超額準備9,824億台幣。
 
 
    **RP資金調度不難**  
    
    債市附買回(RP)市場方面，交易員表示，受颱風休假，且今日適逢季底影響，今日RP市
場較為忙亂，不過利率未見走揚，仍維持上周五調整後的水準。
    
    一證券商交易員指出，由於累積了周一與周二的交易，單子比較多，不過大部分都有續
，縱然有到期未續者，資金也蠻好找的。
    
    〞累積了兩天，次級還有初級都疊在一起。〞一位大型證券商交易員說。    
    
    今日有鴻海&lt;2317.TW&gt;90億台幣公司債、玉山銀行37.5億金融債、元大銀行14.5億金融
債、日本瑞穗銀行5.38億美元30年美元債、遠東商銀30億台幣金融債以及華泰銀6.6億金融
債交割。
    
    本周資金變化因子尚有周五遠東新&lt;1402.TW&gt;52億台幣公司債交割。   
    
    今日證券商10天期公債的附買回利率主要成交在0.43-0.45%；10天期以上公司債RP主要
成交在0.53-0.55%。 
    
    大型票券商與金融機構承作的極短天期公債附買回利率區間落在0.38-0.39%；一周公債
附買回利率區間則落在0.41-0.43%；極短天期公司債RP利率區間則落在0.40-0.41%，一周公
司債附買回利率區間則落在0.44-0.48%；債券附買回成交利率高低與票券商條件及承作對象
不同，有所差異。(完)     

 (審校 曾祥進)

roger.tung.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))</body></xhtml></inlineXML></contentSet></newsItem></Data></ContentItem></Body></ContentEnvelope>

qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:00.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL3N1206F4</altId><language tag="ko" /><subject qcode="N2:STX" /><subject qcode="N2:DBT" /><subject qcode="N2:FRX" /><subject qcode="N2:KR" /><subject qcode="N2:LKO" /><subject qcode="N2:MKTREP" /><subject qcode="N2:REP" /><subject qcode="N2:EMRG" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>9월 수출 8.3% 감소, 시장 전망치 상회..무역수지 89억달러 흑자</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    서울, 10월1일 (로이터) - 9월 수출이 시장 전망치를 상회했다.
    
    산업통상자원부가 1일 발표한 9월 수출은 435억700만 달러를 기록해 지난해 같은 기간에 비해 8.3% 줄어들었다.
    
    로이터통신이 17개 기관을 대상으로 설문조사한 결과 수출은 전년 동기 대비 10.0% 감소할 것으로 예상되면서 전망치를 웃돌았다.
    
    다만 수입은 시장 전망치인 18.1%를 하회했다.
    
    산업부에 따르면 수입은 전년 동기 대비 21.8% 감소한 345억6400 만달러로 집계됐다.
    
    한편 올해 1월부터 지속된 수출과 수입의 동반 감소세는 9월까지 이어졌다.
    
    무역수지는 89억4300만달러를 기록해 44개월 연속 흑자를 기록했다.
    
    (박예나 기자, 편집 이경호 기자)

qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:01.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:00:01.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL3N12026Y</altId><language tag="en" /><subject qcode="N2:BANK" /><subject qcode="N2:REAL" /><subject qcode="N2:HOME" /><subject qcode="N2:MCE" /><subject qcode="N2:ECI" /><subject qcode="N2:REGS" /><subject qcode="N2:AU" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:HOSAL" /><subject qcode="N2:REAM" /><subject qcode="N2:FINS" /><subject qcode="N2:BISV" /><subject qcode="N2:BSVC" /><subject qcode="N2:HBLD" /><subject qcode="N2:CYCS" /><subject qcode="N2:CYCP" /><subject qcode="N2:BACT" /><subject qcode="N2:LEN" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>Australia city home prices rise 0.9 pct in Sept -RPData</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    SYDNEY, Oct 1 (Reuters) - Growth in home prices across
Australia&apos;s capital cities picked up pace in September but
Sydney came to a near standstill in a sign the hot property
market there might be cooling. 
    Thursday&apos;s figures from property consultant CoreLogic RP
Data showed dwelling prices across the major cities climbed 0.9
percent in September, speeding up from 0.3 percent in August.
    Annual growth in home values accelerated to 11.0 percent,
from 10.2 percent in August. Again, the headline numbers masked
wide divisions between cities.
    For September alone, Sydney prices edged up a mere 0.1
percent, while Melbourne rose 2.4 percent. After declines in
August, Canberra bounced back with a 1.0 percent increase, and
Perth rose 0.5 percent.
    RPData head of research Tim Lawless said the slower
month-on-month reading for Sydney came at a time when auction
clearance rates have slipped to the low 70-percent range and the
number of advertised properties has risen. 
    &quot;Vendors are still enjoying strong selling conditions, but
it looks like buyers are slowly regaining some leverage in what
has been a very hot market,&quot; he said.
    &quot;While half of Australia&apos;s capital cities have seen values
rise over the past quarter and year, the other half did not fare
as well.&quot;
    Indeed, Sydney and Melbourne boasted annual gains of 16.7
percent and 14.2 percent respectively, but Perth, Darwin and
Adelaide were in the red led by a 3.9 percent fall for Darwin.
    Sydney has the highest median dwelling price of A$785,000 
($549,578), followed by Melbourne&apos;s A$580,000, which equals the
median price for the combined eight capital cities.
    Regulators have reacted to the bullish conditions in Sydney
and Melbourne by tightening lending standards for property
investment with the aim of keeping annual growth in investment
lending at 10 percent or less.
    There are signs that these measures were working and recent
data showed growth in credit advanced for housing investment
eased to an annual rate of 10.7 percent in August, cooling from
11.1 percent in June, which was the fastest pace in eight years.
($1 = A$1.4284)

 (Reporting by Ian Chua; Editing by Eric Meijer)
 ((ian.chua@thomsonreuters.com; +61 2 9321 8174; RM:
ian.chua.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    Oct 1 (Reuters) -    
    For other diaries, please see:
    U.S. Federal Reserve          [FED/DIARY]
    Polling unit diary            [POLL/DIARY]

    Political and general news    [POL/DIARY]
    Index of all diaries          [IND/DIARY]
    Major central bank events     [CEN/DIARY]
    
    
 ** This Diary is filed daily **
 -----------------------------------------------------------

 THURSDAY, OCTOBER 1

 WASHINGTON - European Central Bank chief Mario Draghi speaks on
the occasion of the awarding of the Atlantic Council Global
Citizens Award - 1330 GMT.
 PRAGUE - European Central Bank banking supervision chief
Daniele Nouy speaks at the ESE Conference 2015 &quot;Financial
supervision in Europe - on the right track?&quot; organized by
Deutsche Bundesbank - 1110 GMT.
 FRANKFURT - German Bundesbank Board member Joachim Nagel to
speak on refinancing of banks from a Central Bank perspective -
1515 GMT.   
 SALT LAKE CITY, United States - Federal Reserve Bank of San
Francisco President John Williams speaks on the economic outlook
before a Salt Lake Area community leader&apos;s event - 1830 GMT.
 ZURICH - Swiss Central Bank Vice Chairman Fritz Zurbruegg
addresses a congress of KOF economic research institute - 1600
GMT.
 OSLO - Central Bank of Norway Governor Oystein Olsen addresses
the Center for Monetary Economics (CME)/ Bi-Norwegian Business
School.
 DUBLIN - 11th Annual Central Bank Conference on Microstructure
of Financial Markets (to Oct. 2). Central bank of Ireland
Governor Patrick Honohan will deliver opening remarks.   

 FRIDAY, OCTOBER 2

 BOSTON - Federal Reserve Bank of Boston President Eric
Rosengren gives welcome and opening remarks before the &quot;Macro
Prudential Monetary Policy&quot; conference hosted by the Federal
Reserve Bank of Boston - 1230 GMT.
 BOSTON - Federal Reserve Bank of Boston President Eric
Rosengren is presenter and Federal Reserve Bank of Minneapolis
President Narayana Kocherlakota is panelist in &quot;Should U.S.
Monetary Policy have a Ternary Mandate?&quot; discussion before the
&quot;Macro Prudential Monetary Policy&quot; conference hosted by the
Federal Reserve Bank of Boston - 1300 GMT.
 WASHINGTON - U.S. Treasury Secretary Jack Lew speaks on fall
fiscal issues before Financial Services Roundtable member CEOs,
in Washington - 1200 GMT.   
 NEW YORK - Federal Reserve Bank of St. Louis President James
Bullard speaks before an event hosted by the Manhattan Institute
for Policy Research - 1300 GMT.
 BOSTON - Federal Reserve Bank of Cleveland President Loretta
Mester participates in panel, &quot;Micro Prudential Versus Macro
Prudential: Problems with Supervisory Control&quot; before the &quot;Macro
Prudential Monetary Policy&quot; conference hosted by the Federal
Reserve Bank of Boston - 1500 GMT.
 BOSTON - Federal Reserve Vice Chair Stanley Fischer speaks
before the &quot;Macro prudential Monetary Policy&quot; conference hosted
by the Federal Reserve Bank of Boston - 1700 GMT.

 SATURDAY, OCTOBER 3

 BOSTON - Federal Reserve Bank of New York President William
Dudley discusses &quot;Is the Active Use of Macroprudential Tools
Institutionally Realistic?&quot; before the &quot;Macroprudential Monetary
Policy&quot; conference hosted by the Federal Reserve Bank of Boston
in Boston - 1500 GMT.

 SUNDAY, OCTOBER 4

 LONDON - FT Africa Summit 2015 (to Oct. 5). Central bank of
Nigeria Governor Godwin Emefiele will be speaking at the summit.
         
    
 MONDAY, OCTOBER 5

 LUXEMBOURG - Eurogroup meeting in Luxembourg.

 TUESDAY, OCTOBER 6

 LIMA - International Monetary Fund holds press briefing on the
World Economic Outlook - 1400 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Ensuring Inclusive Development: Good Practices in Promoting
Accountability in Latin America&quot; - 1700 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Labor Market&apos;s Impact from the Slowdown in Latin America&quot; -
1900 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank holds Youth
Dialogue - 2030 GMT.
 LIMA - World Bank holds a discussion on Social Inclusion:
WikiStage and World Bank Group Lima Special Event - 2200 GMT.
Speakers:- World Bank President Jim Yong Kim and World Bank
Managing Director Sri Mulyani Indrawati.
 SAN FRANCISCO - Federal Reserve Bank of San Francisco President
John Williams speaks on the economic outlook before the Urban
Land Institute Fall Meeting - 2130 GMT.
 LUXEMBOURG - Meeting of Economic and Financial Affairs Council
(ECOFIN).
 SYDNEY - Reserve Bank of Australia holds interest rate meeting
- 0330 GMT.
 TOKYO - Bank of Japan holds monetary policy meeting (to Oct.
7).

 WEDNESDAY, OCTOBER 7

 LIMA - The International Monetary Fund holds a press briefing
on Global Financial Stability Report - 1400 GMT.
 LIMA - The IMF holds a discussion on &quot;Capacity Development in
Latin America and the Caribbean and the Way Forward&quot; - 1430 GMT.
Speakers: IMF Deputy Managing Director Carla Grasso and Central
Bank of Jamaica Governor Brian Wynter. 
 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on &quot;Flagship: Inequality,
Opportunity and Prosperity&quot; - 1500 GMT.
 LIMA - The IMF holds a press briefing on Fiscal Monitor- 1530
GMT.
 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on Ideas for Action: Youth
Engagement for Financing the Future of Development - 1600 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund holds a discussion on
&quot;Bridging the Pacific: Harnessing the Benefits of Rising Trade
and Financial Integration Between Asia and Latin America&quot; - 1630
GMT. Speakers:- IMF First Deputy Managing Director David Lipton
and People Bank of China Deputy Governor Yi Gang.
 LIMA - World Bank holds a discussion on &quot;Building on Peru&apos;s
Success: Boosting Productivity for Faster Growth&quot; - 1715 GMT.
Speakers: World Bank President Jin Yong Kim, Peru Finance
Minister Alonso Segura and Polish Finance Minister Mateusz
Szczurek.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund holds a Conversation on
Climate Change - 1900 GMT. Speakers: IMF Managing Director
Christine Lagarde and World Bank President Jim Yong Kim. 
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund holds a discussion &quot;Energy
Pricing-Getting it Right&quot; - 2030 GMT. Speakers: IMF Deputy
Managing Director Min Zhu and former Irish President Mary
Robinson.    
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund Managing Director Christine
Lagarde and World Bank President Jim Yong Kim participates in a
Town hall meeting - 2230 GMT.
 LONDON - Bank of England holds Monetary Policy Committee (MPC)
meeting (to Oct. 8).
 TOKYO - Bank of Japan announces rate decision - 0200 GMT.
 FRANKFURT - European Central Bank Governing Council meeting. No
interest rate announcements scheduled.
 COPENHAGEN - Danish Economic Councils will publish the
bi-annual report with forecasts of the Danish economy - 1000
GMT.
    
 THURSDAY, OCTOBER 8

 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on &quot;Financial Inclusion: Can
It Meet Multiple Macroeconomic Goals?&quot; - 1500 GMT. Speakers:-
IMF Deputy Managing Director Min Zhu and Reserve Bank of India
Governor Raghuram Rajan.
 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on &quot;Fragility in Middle Income
Countries: New Ideas for Unique Challenges&quot; - 1500 GMT.
 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on &quot;Infrastructure: Investing
for Growth, Investing for People&quot; - 1530 GMT. Speakers:- World
Bank Chief Financial Officer Bertrand Badre, World Bank Managing
Director Sri Mulyani Indrawati and Ivory Coast Finance Minister
Niale Kaba.
 LIMA - IMF/World Bank discussion on &quot;Latin America in the
Spotlight: New Challenges for Central Banking in Latin America&quot;
- 1645 GMT. Speakers:- Bank of England Deputy Governor Nemat
Shafik, Central Bank of Brazil Governor Alexandre Tombini,
Central Bank of Peru Governor Julio Velarde and Central Bank of
Chile President Rodrigo Vergara.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund Managing Director Christine
Lagarde, Bank of England Governor Mark Carney and Brazilian
Finance Minister Joaquim Levy participate in discussion on the
global economy - 1800 GMT. 
 LIMA - World Bank President Jim Yong Kim holds news conference
- 1500 GMT.    
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Solutions for the Solutions Bank?&quot; - 1800 GMT.
 LIMA - World Bank President Jim Yong Kim participates in a
discussion titled &quot;Young Entrepreneurs as Drivers of Sustainable
Growth&quot; - 1900 GMT.  
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Growth and Inclusion in Latin America: the Next Decade&quot; - 1930
GMT. Speakers:- IMF Deputy Managing Director Mitsuhiro Furusawa,
Central Bank Peru former Governor Richard Webb and Peru Finance
Minister Alonso Segura.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;The Financial System We Want: Reshaping Finance for Sustainable
Development&quot; - 2000 GMT. Speakers:- Bank of England Governor
Mark Carney, Central Bank of Bangladesh Governor Atiur Rahman, 
People&apos;s Bank of China Deputy Governor Yi Gang and Central Bank
of Brazil Governor Alexandre Tombini - 2000 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Mobilizing Financing for Private Investment - 2100 GMT.
 LIMA - World Bank President Jim Yong Kim participates in
discussion on &quot;Future of Food: A Conversation about Shaping a
Climate-Smart Food System&quot; - 2130 GMT.
 LIMA - G-24 members hold news conference - 2230 GMT.
 MANKATO, United States - Federal Reserve Bank of Minneapolis
President Narayana Kocherlakota gives welcome remarks and
participates in forum before the Greater Mankato Growth Event -
1700 GMT.
 WASHINGTON - U.S. Federal Open Market Committee will publish
the minutes of September policy meeting - 1800 GMT.
 SPOKANE, United States - Federal Reserve Bank of San Francisco
President John Williams speaks on the economic outlook before
the Spokane Metropolitan Area Business and Community Leaders
Luncheon - 1930 GMT.          
 LONDON - Bank of England announces interest rate decision -
1100 GMT.          
 LONDON - Bank of England will publish the minutes of interest
rate meeting - 1100 GMT.                
 ST LOUIS - Federal Reserve Bank of St. Louis President James
Bullard gives welcome remarks before the Children&apos;s Saving
Account Symposium hosted by the Federal Reserve Bank of St.
Louis - 1330 GMT.  
    
 FRIDAY, OCTOBER 9 
    
 LIMA - G-20 members hold news conference - 1330 GMT. 
 LIMA - World Bank holds a discussion on &quot;Unleashing Private
Investment in Renewable Energy&quot; - 1600 GMT. Speakers:- World
Bank President Jim Yong Kim and Norway Foreign Minister Borge
Brende.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Combating Illicit Financial Flows: Turning Commitments into
Action&quot; - 1600 GMT.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund Middle East and Central Asia
department holds news conference - 1615 GMT. 
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Structural Reforms, Inequality, and Growth&quot; - 1630 GMT.
Speakers:- IMF Deputy Managing Director Min Zhu, Mexico Finance
Minister Luis Videgaray, South African Finance Minister Nhlanhla
Nene and Eurogroup President Jeroen Dijsselbloem.
 LIMA - International Monetary Fund/World Bank discussion on
&quot;Managing the Volatility of Commodity Revenues: Fiscal Policy
Responses&quot; - 1730 GMT. Speakers:- IMF Deputy Managing Director
Mitsuhiro Furusawa, Chile Finance Minister Rodrigo Valdes and
Angola Finance Minister Armando Manuel.
 MILWAUKEE, United States - Federal Reserve Bank of Chicago
President Charles Evans speaks on current economic conditions
and monetary policy before the CFA Society Milwaukee &quot;Economics
and Monetary Policy Update&quot; - 1730 GMT.   
 NEW YORK - Federal Reserve Bank of Atlanta President Dennis
Lockhart speaks before the Society of American Business Editors
and Writers (SABEW) Fall Conference - 1310 GMT.   
 VIENNA - National Bank of Austria chief Ewald Nowotny speaks at
a business journalists event - 0800 GMT.
    
 SATURDAY, OCTOBER 10   
    
 LIMA - Bank of Canada Governor Stephen Poloz will give a speech
at the Institute of International Finance - 0645 GMT.   
    
 MONDAY, OCTOBER 12
    
 WASHINGTON - Bank of Canada Governor Stephen Poloz is scheduled
to make a luncheon speech at the National Association for
Business Economics.
 ORLANDO, United States - Federal Reserve Bank of Atlanta
President Dennis Lockhart speaks before the AUBER Fall
Conference - 1210 GMT

    RUGBY 
    WORLD CUP (to Oct. 31)
    MATCHES
    Wales v Fiji
    Buoyant Welsh seek to build on momentum
    CARDIFF - Wales return to the Millennium Stadium to face
Fiji in Pool A looking to build on their epic victory over
England at Twickenham and close on the quarter-finals. (RUGBY
UNION-WORLD/WALES-FIJI expect by 1745 GMT/1:45PM ET, by Ed
Osmond, Nick Mulvenney and Martyn Herman, 400 words)
    We will also file quotes sidebars on merit.
    - -
    France v Canada
    France call on flair for plucky Canucks
    MILTON KEYNES - Unbeaten France change tack for an 
expansive, free-flowing game against a lively Canadian side that
came so close to upsetting Italy. (RUGBY
UNION-WORLD/FRANCE-CANADA expect by 2200 GMT/6:00PM ET, by
Justin Palmer, 400 words)
    - -
    TEAM NEWS
    England name team to face Australia
    Jonathan Joseph is expected to return to the starting side
as England look to score tries against Australia on Saturday.
(RUGBY UNION-WORLD/ENGLAND-TEAM,(PIX, TV) expect by 1200 GMT/8
AM ET, by Mitch Phillips, 400 words).
    
    Australia name side for England clash
    Australia are expected to be at full strength when they
unveil their team to face England at Twickenham. (RUGBY
UNION-WORLD/AUSTRALIA-TEAM, (PIX), expect by 0900GMT/5AM ET, by
Nick Mulvenney, 400 words)
    
    Scotland name team to face Springboks
    Scotland will name the team to face the Springboks on
Saturday with an injury concern still hanging over their main
playmaker Finn Russell.
(RUGBY UNION-WORLD/SCOTLAND-TEAM,(PIX, TV) expect by 1200GMT/8AM
ET, by John Geddie, 400 words plus sidebars.
    - -
    PREVIEWS
    New Zealand v Georgia
    Georgia relish first game against All Blacks
    CARDIFF - Georgia are excited about facing world champions
New Zealand for the first time in Pool C on Friday and are ready
to put their bodies on the line in a damage limitation exercise.
(RUGBY UNION-WORLD/NEWZEALAND-GEORGIA (PREVIEW), moved, by Ed
Osmond, 400 words)
    - -
    England v Australia
    LONDON - The second big showdown from Pool A sees England
desperately needing to beat Australia keep their quarter-final
hopes alive. (RUGBY UNION-WORLD/ENGLAND-AUSTRALIA (PREVIEW),
expect by 1900 GMT/3 PM, by Mitch Phillips, 400 words.
    
    Samoa v Japan
    LONDON - After beating South Africa but then losing to
Scotland, Japan need to overcome the physical challenge of Samoa
to retain their dream of a first appearance in the
quarter-finals. (RUGBY UNION-WORLD/SAMOA-JAPAN (PREVIEW), expect
by 1300 GMT/9 AM, by Justin Palmer, 400 words.
    
    South Africa v Scotland
    Springboks in fight for World Cup survival against Scotland
    LONDON - Twice world champions South Africa, damaged by
their shock defeat by Japan, must beat a resurgent Scotland in
their crunch game on Saturday to lower the odds on an
ignominious early Rugby World Cup exit. (RUGBY
UNION-WORLD/SAFRICA-SCOTLAND (PREVIEW), expect by 15:45
GMT/11:45 AM ET, by Angus MacSwan, 400 words)
    - -
    INTERVIEW
    England must forget Wales and focus on Australia - Johnson
    LONDON - England&apos;s players must wipe Wales from their minds
and focus entirely on Australia to keep their tournament hopes
alive, says former captain and world champion Martin Johnson who
has experienced the highs and lows of the tournament as player
and coach. (RUGBY UNION-WORLD/ENGLAND-JOHNSON (INTERVIEW),
moved, by Mitch Phillips, 500 words)
    - -
    FEATURE
    England look to Marseille 2007 for inspiration
    LONDON - England&apos;s do or die Pool A match against Australia
on Saturday revives memories of the 2007 quarter-final when they
hauled themselves off the canvas to stun the Wallabies en route
to the final. (RUGBY UNION-WORLD/ENGLAND-2007 (FEATURE, PIX),
moved, by Mitch Phillips, 650 words)
    - -    
    We will also monitor news from across the tournament and
file stories throughout. (RUGBY UNION-WORLD/, expect throughout)
    - - - - 
    BASEBALL
    Cardinals eye third straight NL Central crown
    The St. Louis Cardinals will try to clinch their third
consecutive National League Central championship when they visit
the Pittsburgh Pirates for a double-header. (BASEBALL-PIRATES,
expect by 0300 GMT/11 PM ET, by The Sports Xchange, 400 words)
    - -
    Jays visit Orioles with chance clinch AL East
    The Toronto Blue Jays will try to win their first American
League East title since 1993 when they visit the Baltimore
Orioles. (BASEBALL-ORIOLES/, expect by 0200 GMT/9 PM ET, by The
Sports Xchange, 400 words)
    - -
    Stroman guides Toronto to AL East title
    Marcus Stroman allowed one run in eight strong innings as
the Toronto Blue Jays clinched their first American League East
title in 22 years with a 15-2 victory over the Baltimore Orioles
in the first game of a double header. (BASEBALL-HIGHLIGHTS/,
moved with updates to follow, 800 words)
    - - - -
    SOCCER
    Previews
    Premier League
    Wenger, Rodgers under scrutiny ahead of clashes with rivals 
    LONDON - Arsene Wenger may be under pressure after their
Champions League traumas but his fourth-placed side can go level
on points with leaders Manchester United by beating them on
Sunday while under-fire Liverpool boss Brendan Rodgers takes his
struggling side to rivals Everton. (SOCCER-ENGLAND/ (PREVIEW),

qcode="R:KRIMP=ECI" /><subject qcode="R:KRTBLP=ECI" /><headline>TABLE-S.Korea Sept exports fall 8.3 pct y/y, better than expected</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    SEOUL, Oct 1 (Reuters) - Following are South Korea&apos;s
preliminary export and import figures for September, released by
the Ministry of Trade, Industry and Energy on Thursday
(rounded):
                                   SEPT       *AUG
 Balance ($ billion)                8.9        4.3
 Exports ($ billion)               43.5       39.2
         (pct growth vs yr ago)    -8.3      -14.9
 Imports ($ billion)               34.6       35.0
         (pct growth vs yr ago)   -21.8      -18.3
 * Revised figures released on Sept. 15 [ID:nL4N11K349]
    NOTES:
    - Reuters poll: Exports were seen down 10.0 percent in
September over a year earlier while imports were seen down 18.1
percent. [ID:nL4N11V07Y]
    - The average export value per working day stood at $2.02
billion in September, compared with a revised $1.78 billion in
August, Thomson Reuters calculations show. 
    - China is South Korea&apos;s largest export market, taking about
one-quarter of shipments, followed by the United States and the
European Union.   
    - By product, electronics goods account for over one-fifth
of the country&apos;s total exports, followed chemical products and
industrial machinery.

 (Reporting by Christine Kim; Editing by Choonsik Yoo)
 ((christine.kim@thomsonreuters.com; 822 3704 5665; Reuters
Messaging: christine.kim.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

 THURSDAY, OCTOBER 1

 PRAGUE - European Central Bank banking supervision chief
Daniele Nouy speaks at the ESE Conference 2015 &quot;Financial

contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    Oct 1 (Reuters) - Korea South-East Power Co Ltd (KOSEP)
[KOSEP.UL] is seeking 58,000 tonnes of semi-anthracite or
anthracite coal for shipment between November and December via a
spot tender, the utility said on its website (http://www.kosep.co.kr).
    The tender will close at 3 p.m.(0600 GMT) on October 14, and
other details are as follows:
    
    TONNES     SPECIFICATION (NAR)     DELIVERY SCHEDULE
    58,000     min. 6,300kcal/kg       November 25-December 25
    
    * Note: NAR stands for Net As Received, and each shipment of
coal should be supplied from a single mine.
    

 (Reporting by Rebecca Jang; Editing by Michael Perry)
 ((rebecca.jang@thomsonreuters.com;))

DIGEST- British Business - Oct 1</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    Oct 1 (Reuters) - The following are the top stories on the
business pages of British newspapers. Reuters has not verified
these stories and does not vouch for their accuracy.
        
    The Times
    Britain has grown faster than any other leading economy
since 2013 after bouncing back from recession far more strongly
than had been thought, according to data published by the Office
of National Statistics. (http://thetim.es/1MHlZUd)
    
    Begbies Traynor Group PLC &lt;BEG.L&gt;, the London-listed
insolvency firm, has bought the assets of its regional rival P&amp;A
Partnership out of administration. (http://thetim.es/1MHnTUF)
    
    The Guardian
    Paul Fisher, deputy head of the Bank of England&apos;s regulatory
arm, has warned of the risk of bowing to pressure from lobbyists
in the banking industry who want to see a relaxation of rules
introduced since the banking crisis. (http://bit.ly/1MHmUUo)

     Tony Hayward, chairman of Glencore PLC &lt;GLEN.L&gt;, has put
his hand in his pocket to buy some shares. He&apos;s splashed out the
mighty sum of, well, nearly 91,000 pounds ($137,601.10).  (http://bit.ly/1MHn7XR)
    
     The Telegraph
    The Institute of Directors, which represents thousands of
top bosses across Britain, slammed Transport for London&apos;s plans
to ban many of Uber&apos;s key features, saying they would &quot;embed
economic inefficiency&quot; in the capital&apos;s transport regulation. (http://bit.ly/1MHnYb2)
    
    The divide between house prices in the North and South of
England has hit a record high, exceeding 150,000 pounds for the
first time. Average prices in the South are now more than twice
as high as those in the North - at 303,811 pounds and 150,851
pounds respectively - according to the latest Nationwide House
Price Index. (http://bit.ly/1MHo823)
    
    Sky News
    The electrification of two rail lines, TransPennine Express
Railway between Manchester and York and the Midland Mainline
from London to Sheffield, which will lead to quicker journey
times for thousands of passengers, is to go ahead after being
stopped earlier this year. (http://bit.ly/1MHog1A)
    
    Glasgow-based Home Energy and Lifestyle Management has been
fined 200,000 pounds by the Information Commissioner&apos;s Office
after making more than six million automated calls offering
&apos;free&apos; solar panels. (http://bit.ly/1MHouWr)
    
    The Independent
    Online supermarket Ocado Group PLC &lt;OCDO.L&gt; has angered its
customers by announcing it will be charging 5 pence for grocery
bags, without giving shoppers the chance to opt out. (http://ind.pn/1MHoANK)
    
 ($1 = 0.6613 pounds)

 (Compiled by Parikshit Mishra in Bengaluru)

xmlns:rtr="http://www.reuters.com/ns/2003/08/content" xmlns:x="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><catalogRef href="http://www.iptc.org/std/catalog/catalog.IPTC-G2-Standards_14.xml" /><itemMeta><itemClass qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:04:28.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:04:28.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL1N1203JZ</altId><language tag="en" /><subject qcode="N2:DBT" /><subject qcode="N2:PR1" /><subject qcode="N2:MUNI" /><subject qcode="N2:BISV" /><subject qcode="N2:INVS" /><subject qcode="N2:DBTR" /><subject qcode="N2:REORG" /><subject qcode="N2:ISU" /><subject qcode="N2:PR" /><subject qcode="N2:US" /><subject qcode="N2:NEWS1" /><subject qcode="N2:GFIN" /><subject qcode="N2:BINS" /><subject qcode="N2:AMERS" /><subject qcode="N2:LATAM" /><subject qcode="N2:FINS" /><subject qcode="N2:BACT" /><subject qcode="N2:FIND1" /><subject qcode="N2:MEVN" /><subject qcode="N2:GEN" /><subject qcode="N2:POL" /><subject qcode="N2:LEN" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>Puerto Rico, bondholders start restructuring talks over financing arm -source</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    NEW YORK, Sept 30 (Reuters) - Debt restructuring talks over
Puerto Rico&apos;s financing arm, the Government Development Bank,
have begun between a group of bondholders and the bank, a source
familiar with the situation said, after the creditors signed
non-disclosure agreements earlier on Wednesday.
    GDB chief Melba Acosta said last week the bank would be the
next entity from the commonwealth to engage in restructuring
negotiations, following utility PREPA, which came to a deal with
bondholders in September after about a year of talks.
[ID:nL1N11U1B3]
    Puerto Rico officials earlier in September proposed
restructuring $18 billion of debt due in the coming five years
as part of a broad plan to pull the island out of financial
crisis.
    The bondholders started negotiations on Wednesday, after the
non-disclosure agreements were signed earlier in the day, said
the source, who requested anonymity because the talks are not
public. It will probably take several days to see whether
negotiations can progress, the source said. 
    Some investors, or potential investors, which were not
necessarily in that group, had already signed non-disclosures
last week, a separate source familiar with the situation
previously said. [ID:nL1N11U1B3]
    Signing non-disclosure agreements restricts bondholders from
disclosing non-public information and from trading and opens the
way to formal negotiations.
    Bloomberg earlier Wednesday reported the talks had started.
    The GDB bondholder group consists of investment funds
Brigade, Fir Tree, Solus, Fore Research &amp; Management, Avenue
Capital, Candlewood, and Claren Road, sources previously said.
[ID:nL1N11U1B3]
    The individual funds either did not respond for comment or
declined to comment on Wednesday. A spokeswoman for the GDB
declined to comment.
    Debt restructuring could take the form of a debt exchange
with new capital added. That could include exchanging notes for
notes in The Puerto Rico Infrastructure Financing Authority
(PRIFA) which could be backed by oil revenues, a source familiar
with the situation said last week. [ID:nL1N11U1B3]
    

 (Reporting by Megan Davies)
 ((megan.davies@thomsonreuters.com; +1 646 223 6190;))

　レアルは前半２９分、それまで相手の守備に抑えられ気味だったクリスティアノ・ロナルドがイスコのパスから先制点を奪取。マルメが後半３３分に退場者を出して試合の趨勢が決まると、終了間際にもロナルドが追加点を奪った。

　すでにＣＬ歴代最多得点者となっていたロナウドはその数字を８２得点まで伸ばすと、ラウルの持つクラブ通算歴代最多３２３得点の記録に肩を並べた。

　同組のパリ・サンジェルマン（フランス、ＰＳＧ）は敵地でシャフタル・ドネツク（ウクライナ）に３─０で快勝。前半にダビドルイスらのゴールで２点をリードすると、終了間際にはオウンゴールで加点した。

　Ｃ組のアトレチコ・マドリード（スペイン）はホームでベンフィカ（ポルトガル）に１─２と黒星。ガラタサライ（トルコ）とアスタナ（カザフスタン）は２─２で引き分けた。</body></xhtml></inlineXML></contentSet></newsItem></Data></ContentItem></Body></ContentEnvelope>

/><rtr:versionedId guid="20151001-000650000-nL1N1203NZ-1-2" /><TakeSequence>1</TakeSequence></itemMeta><contentMeta><urgency>3</urgency><altId type="idType:USN" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL1N1203NZ</altId><language tag="en" /><subject qcode="N2:EMRG" /><subject qcode="N2:VE" /><subject qcode="N2:LATAM" /><subject qcode="N2:MCE" /><subject qcode="N2:OILG" /><subject qcode="N2:AMERS" /><subject qcode="N2:INFL" /><subject qcode="N2:POL" /><subject qcode="N2:ENER" /><subject qcode="N2:ECI" /><subject qcode="N2:GEN" /><subject qcode="N2:LEN" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>Venezuela revises 2014 data to show economy shrank 4 percent </headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    CARACAS, Sept 30 (Reuters) - Venezuela&apos;s government has
revised its economic data for 2014, showing that Gross Domestic
Product (GDP) declined 4.0 percent in the worst performance
around Latin America, according to a filing on Wednesday in the
United States.
    President Nicolas Maduro had said earlier this year that GDP
shrank 3 percent last year. 
    The government has given no GDP data for 2015, to the anger
of opponents and consternation of economists.
    In its filing to the U.S. Securities and Exchange
Commission, the Maduro government said the OPEC nation&apos;s
petroleum sector expanded 0.3 percent last year, whereas the
non-petroleum sector decreased 3.8 percent. (http://1.usa.gov/1j1qteQ)
    Inflation was 68.5 percent.
    Most economists predict a similar or worse GDP performance
this year, with even higher inflation.
    Venezuela makes the filing to the SEC because it is an
issuer of dollar-denominated bonds. 
    Maduro says domestic political foes and opposition-aligned
businessmen have been deliberately sabotaging Venezuela&apos;s
economy via hoarding, price-gouging, smuggling and other means.
    But critics say 16 years of hardline socialist policies,
including price and currency controls plus hostility toward the
private sector, are behind Venezuela&apos;s economic woes.
    The plunge in oil prices, which account for 96 percent of
hard-currency revenues, has also hit Venezuela hard.
    Imports plunged to $32.15 billion last year, compared with
$53.02 billion in 2013, according to the filing. 
    Export revenue dropped to $60.50 billion in 2014 from $88.96
billion the previous year.
    The filing confirmed ally China had loaned Venezuela more
than $55 billion since 2007 in loans to be repaid with oil
shipments. 
    &quot;The Republic agreed a U.S.$10.0 billion loan with China in
March 2015, and a further U.S.$5.0 billion loan with China in
September 2015, to be used to finance oil projects,&quot; it added of
the most recent components of that total.  

 (Reporting by Eyanir Chinea and Andrew Cawthorne; Editing by
Lisa Shumaker)
 ((andrew.cawthorne@thomsonreuters.com)(+58 212 277
2655)(Reuters Messaging:
andrew.cawthorne.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net)(Twitter:
@ReutersVzla))

Keywords: VENEZUELA ECONOMY/</body></xhtml></inlineXML></contentSet></newsItem></Data></ContentItem></Body></ContentEnvelope>

الانباءالساعة 0001 بتوقيت جرينتش اليوم الخميس</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    واشطن أول أكتوبر تشرين الأول (رويترز) - قال وزير الخارجية
الامريكي جون كيري ان المحادثات العسكرية بين الولايات المتحدة
وروسيا قد تبدأ في وقت قريب ربما اليوم الخميس لضمان عدم نشوب صراع
دون قصد اثناء الضربات الجوية التي يشنها البلدان في سوريا.
    
    المنامة - قالت وزارة الداخلية البحرينية إن قوات الأمن اكتشفت
مصنعا ضخما لتصنيع القنابل وألقت القبض على عدد الاشخاص يشتبه بان
لهم صلات بالحرس الثوري الإيراني.
                                                            
    بروكسل - قال حلف شمال الاطلسي انه قلق من ان الضربات الجوية
الروسية في سوريا ربما دمرت مناطق في البلاد تسيطر عليها المعارضة
وانها ربما لم تستهدف مواقع تنظيم الدولة الاسلامية.
    
    الرياض - قال التحالف الذي تقوده السعودية إن قواته التي تقاتل
الحوثيين المدعومين من إيران في اليمن احتجزت قاربا إيرانيا محملا
بالسلاح في بحر العرب كان في طريقه لليمن لتسليم شحنته للحوثيين.
    
    الامم المتحدة - اتهم الرئيس الفلسطيني محمود عباس إسرائيل
بتقويض جهود الولايات المتحدة للوساطة من أجل السلام وقال إن
العمليات الأمنية الإسرائيلية في المسجد الأقصى بالقدس قد تؤدي إلى
اندلاع حرب دينية.
    
    موسكو - قالت وزارة الدفاع الروسية إنها نفذت نحو عشرين طلعة
جوية فوق سوريا وقصفت ثمانية أهداف تابعة لتنظيم الدولة الإسلامية.
    
    القاهرة - قال بيان إن قوات الأمن المصرية قتلت أربعة مطلوبين
من أعضاء جماعة الإخوان المسلمين المحظورة في اشتباك بمدينة
الإسكندرية الساحلية.

［東京　１日　ロイター］ - 
    BUZZ-ユーロ／ポンドテクニカル分析：強気シグナル継続、0.7417ポンドが目先の抵抗線
    
    ＊０．４５％安で始まった。欧米株が値を上げるなか、ユーロに売りが出た。
    ＊９月２９日に日足終値が８月高値（０．７４２１ポンド）を上回り、一段高が見込まれたものの、同３０日は下落して終えた。
    ＊モメンタム指標は中立。５日、１０日、２０日移動平均線は上向き。強気の形状。
    ＊５月の高値（０．７４８２ポンド）がターゲット。目先の抵抗線はロンドン市場の高値（０．７４１７ポンド）。    
    ＊目先の支持線はニューヨーク市場の安値（０．７３６１ポンド）、その次は１０日線（０．７３４１ポンド）。
    
    ＊BUZZはコメント・分析サービスで、筆者の個人的見解に基づいて書かれています。

/><subject qcode="N2:CEN" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><headline>〔マーケットアイ〕金利：国債先物が反発で寄り付く、日銀短観は楽観できず</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    ［東京　１日　ロイター］ -   
    ＜０９：００＞　国債先物が反発で寄り付く、日銀短観は楽観できず
    
    国債先物中心限月１２月限は、前日比７銭高の１４８円２３銭と反発して寄り付いた。前日の海外市場で、米債が買われた流れを引き継いだ。ただ、高値警戒感が意識される中で、きょうの１０年債入札を前に、上値を買い進む動きは限られている。
    
    日銀が午前８時５０分に発表した９月短観によると、大企業製造業ＤＩはプラス１２とロイター予測（プラス１３）を下回った。６月短観（プラス１５）から３ポイント悪化した。現時点で相場への影響は限られている。
    市場では「大企業製造業の景況感は悪化したが、事前予想の範囲。ただ、中国景気減速の影響が一部セクターで出ており、先行きは決して楽観できない」（国内金融機関）との見方が出ている。

xmlns:rtr="http://www.reuters.com/ns/2003/08/content" xmlns:x="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><catalogRef href="http://www.iptc.org/std/catalog/catalog.IPTC-G2-Standards_14.xml" /><itemMeta><itemClass qcode="icls:text" /><provider qcode="NS:RTRS" /><versionCreated>2015-10-01T00:08:48.000Z</versionCreated><firstCreated>2015-10-01T00:01:01.000Z</firstCreated><pubStatus qcode="stat:usable" rtr:isOriginal="1">nL3T12100D</altId><language tag="zh" /><subject qcode="N2:MCE" /><subject qcode="N2:ECI" /><subject qcode="N2:EMRG" /><subject qcode="N2:KR" /><subject qcode="N2:ASIA" /><subject qcode="N2:CNEWS" /><subject qcode="N2:LZH" /><subject qcode="N2:RTRS" /><subject qcode="N2:TRACC" /><subject qcode="N2:GEN" /><subject qcode="N2:POL" /><subject qcode="N2:TRD" /><subject qcode="R:0#KRCOMP1=KQ" /><subject qcode="R:KRW=" /><subject qcode="R:KRIMP=ECI" /><subject qcode="R:KREXP=ECI" /><subject qcode="R:KRTBLP=ECI" /><headline>表格：韓國9月出口較上年同期下降8.3%，降幅小於預估</headline></contentMeta><contentSet><inlineXML contenttype="application/xhtml+xml"><xhtml xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"><body>    路透首爾10月1日 - 韓國產業通商資源部周四公布9月進出口與貿易收支初值如下(經四捨五入)：
    
                                      9月       *8月 
    貿易收支(10億美元)                8.9        4.3
    出口(10億美元)                   43.5       39.2
        (較上年同期變動百分比)       -8.3      -14.9
    進口(10億美元)                   34.6       35.0
        (較上年同期變動百分比)      -21.8      -18.3
    
    * 為2015年9月15日公布的修正值
    
    附註：   
    - 路透調查結果為，分析師預測9月出口較上年同期下降10.0%，進口
下降18.1%。
    - 湯森路透計算顯示，9月平均每工作日出口額為20.2億美元，8月修正為17.8億美元。 
    - 中國是韓國最大的出口市場，約占其出口的四分之一，其次是美國和歐盟。
    - 以產品類別分，電子產品是最大出口品，所占比例超五分之一，其次是化學品和工業機械。(完)

Bernie Sanders
of Vermont raised more than $24 million over the last three
months as he wages a populist challenge to become the Democratic
presidential nominee, the New York Times reported on Wednesday.
    Sanders&apos; advisers, in announcing the fund-raising tally on
Wednesday night with several hours to go before the end of the
quarter, also said the senator had more than $25 million in cash
on hand, the Times said.
